Source Buffer Queue processed count (query only). Type\+: A\+Lint

The number of queued buffers that have been fully processed, and can be removed with al\+Source\+Unqueue\+Buffers.

Looping sources will never fully process buffers because they will be set to play again for when the source loops. \index{al.\+h@{al.\+h}!A\+L\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+S\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+ED@{A\+L\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+S\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+ED}}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+C\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+EL}{AL_DISTANCE_MODEL}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+C\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+EL~0x\+D000}\hypertarget{al_8h_a04cb8d5a824c2b49f26523995c4ecd29}{}\label{al_8h_a04cb8d5a824c2b49f26523995c4ecd29}
Distance attenuation model. Type\+: A\+Lint Range\+: \mbox{[}A\+L\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE, A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+E\+R\+S\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+CE, A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+E\+R\+S\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+M\+P\+ED, A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+E\+A\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+CE, A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+E\+A\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+M\+P\+ED, A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+N\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+CE, A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+N\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+M\+P\+ED\mbox{]} Default\+: A\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+E\+R\+S\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+A\+N\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+M\+P\+ED

The model by which sources attenuate with distance.

None -\/ No distance attenuation. Inverse -\/ Doubling the distance halves the source gain. Linear -\/ Linear gain scaling between the reference and max distances. Exponent -\/ Exponential gain dropoff.

Clamped variations work like the non-\/clamped counterparts, except the distance calculated is clamped between the reference and max distances. \index{al.\+h@{al.\+h}!A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+C\+T\+OR@{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+C\+T\+OR}}
\index{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+C\+T\+OR@{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+C\+T\+OR}!al.\+h@{al.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+C\+T\+OR}{AL_DOPPLER_FACTOR}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+C\+T\+OR~0x\+C000}\hypertarget{al_8h_aef68e4f99022c27c2d8fb3f08b44c3e2}{}\label{al_8h_aef68e4f99022c27c2d8fb3f08b44c3e2}
Doppler scale. Type\+: A\+Lfloat Range\+: \mbox{[}0.\+0 -\/ \mbox{]} Default\+: 1.\+0

Scale for source and listener velocities. \index{al.\+h@{al.\+h}!A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+L\+O\+C\+I\+TY@{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+L\+O\+C\+I\+TY}}
\index{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+L\+O\+C\+I\+TY@{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+L\+O\+C\+I\+TY}!al.\+h@{al.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+L\+O\+C\+I\+TY}{AL_DOPPLER_VELOCITY}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+O\+P\+P\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+L\+O\+C\+I\+TY~0x\+C001}\hypertarget{al_8h_a7e6e153f7a5991b675018e881a344c03}{}\label{al_8h_a7e6e153f7a5991b675018e881a344c03}
Doppler velocity (deprecated).

The source or listener location in three dimensional space.

Open\+AL, like Open\+GL, uses a right handed coordinate system, where in a frontal default view X (thumb) points right, Y points up (index finger), and Z points towards the viewer/camera (middle finger).
